 chhattisgarh main farji google image se avaidh tareeke se bani imaaraton ko vaid karne kaa kaam joro par chal rahaa he
 The state government, by issuing an order, started the process of legalizing the construction without permission
 prakriya main tex bharke avaidh nirmaan kaa niyamitikaran kiya janaa tha
 The order said that only the houses built before 30 August 2016 can be regularized
 iske liye avaidh nirmaan kii naap jokh ke saath-saath puure rakabe kaa byora prastut kiya janaa tha
 This condition was also made mandatory that Google images before August 2016 should also be included with the application
 lekin badi taadaad main logon ne 2016 ke baad kiguglaimage lagaakar apana aavedan jamaa kar diya
 The trickery of legalizing thousands of illegal constructions by manipulating the Google image is going on in full swing
 is maamle main do architect or ek engeenior ko nagareey prashasan vibhaag ne notice jari kiya he
 The state's Town and Country Planning Department has received more than one lakh applications to legalize illegal construction across the state
 philhal maatr 18 fisadi prakarnon kaa niraakaran kiya gaya he
 To make them legal, the government has received an amount of 34 crores as penalty
 nagareey prashasan vibhaag ke afasaron kaa daawa he ki 31 march 2018 ke pehle sabhi maamle nipta die jaaenge
 On the other hand, the process of legitimizing illegal construction has given rise to rampant corruption
 vyavsaayik bhawanon , dukaanon , badi imaarte , hotel or vyavsaayik upyog main kiraye par di jane vaali imaaraton ke alaava houseing complex ke kai aise avaidh nirmaan ko vaid banane karne kii prakriya shuru kar di gai he, jo kabhi bhi khatarnaak sabit ho sakati hai
 Many buildings have neither adequate lighting nor any arrangement of fire fighting systems
 iske baavjood unhen jurmaana adaa kar vaidhata pradaan kii ja rahi he
 Town and Country Planning and the Municipal Corporation do not have enough staff to conduct site trials while disposing of cases of applicants
 natijatan khatarnaak or haadason ke andeshe vaale avaidh nirmaan bhi suniyojit rup se vaid ho rahe hai
 Aaj Tak has brought out the biggest survey on the assembly elections of four states
 india today or exis dwaara karaae gaye survey main do rajyon main bijepi kii to ek main congress kii sarkaar banati dikh rahi he, jabaki uttar pradesh main bijepi sabase badi party banakar ubhar rahi he
 First of all talk about Goa, BJP will form government again here
 40 siton main se bijepi ko yahaan 22 se 25 siten mil sakati hai
 The Congress will be in second place, which will get 12 to 14 seats, while the Aam Aadmi Party is expected to get 1 to 2 seats
 goa main 1986 sample liye gaye, jabaki survey 16 se 24 janvari ke bich karaayaa gaya
 The survey has been done jointly
 siem ke liye parrikar pehali pasandgova main mukhyamantri kii rup main raksha mantri manohar parrikar pehali pasand hai
 He is liked by 29 percent people, while the current CM Laxmikant Parsekar is chosen by 16 percent
 vahiin 15 pratishat log chaahate hai ki digambar kaamat mukhyamantri or 4 pratishat logon kii pasand vijay saradesai hai
 Parrikar is the former Chief Minister of Goa
 modi ke kaam se log khushgova ke 50 fisadi logon ne modi sarkaar ke kaam ko acha bataaya he, jabaki 22 fisadi logon ko abhi bhi ummid he, jabaki 28 fisadi logon ne kharaab bataaya he
 The saffron will wave in Uttarakhand as well, and in Uttarakhand, BJP seems to be formed with an absolute majority
 yahambijepico 40 se 44 siten mil rahi hai to sattadhari congress 23 se 27 siton par simat rahi he
 In the 70-seat Uttarakhand, 4130 samples have been taken, while the survey was conducted from 13 to 29 January
 punjab main chalegaa congress kaa jaadoogova-uttarakhand ke baad punjab main congress ko raahat milti dikh rahi hai
 Congress can get 60 to 65 seats, while you will be in second place with 41 to 44 seats

 kya he GM Diet plan?gm Diet matlab general motarsdit programko khaastaur par vajan ghataane ke liye taiyaar kiya gaya he

 Seven Day Plan of GM Diet Day 1: Today you only have to eat fruits but remember that you do not eat bananas
 aap angoor, lichi or aam jaise falon kaa seven kar sakati hai

 Day 3: On the third day you can eat a mixed combo of fruits and vegetables

 Day 4:aaj ke din aapako sirf 6 kele khaane hai or3 se 4 glass doodhpi sakati hai

 aap chahen to shimla mirch, pyaaj, lahasun or tamaato kaa bana soup bhi pi sakati hai

 Day 5:aaj ke din kii shuruyaat healdi sprouts, paneer yaa phir tamaato ke salad ke saath karen

 tamaato kaa seven karne se aapke sharir mempani kii kameepuri hogi

 Day 6:aaj ke din aapako tamaato ko na kahana he

 subjiyan aapke sharir main vitamins or fibre kii kami ko puraa karengi

 Day 7:aaj diet plan kaa aakhri din aaj aapako sharir or man donon halkaa or fresh mahasoos hoga

 saath hi dher sara pani pinaa na bhoolen

 Use of barley in food significantly reduces the level of bad cholesterol responsible for many heart diseases
 haal hi main ek nae adhyayan main is baat kaa pataa chalaa he ki jau main jayee kii tarah hi cholestrol kam karne vaale prabhaav maujuud hote hai
 According to research results, the body can reduce low-density lipoprotein ie LDL and non-high density lipoprotein ie non HDL by seven percent
 canada ke saint mishael hospital se vladimir wooksun ne bataaya, "yah nishkarsh tip-2 madhumeh se peedit logon ke liye behad mahatvapurn he, jinhen hriday rogon kaa jokhim sabase zyada hota he
 LDL cholesterol levels remain normal in such people, but non-hdl or apolipoprotein b levels are high
 " Barley can benefit not only in individuals at high risk of bad cholesterol, but also in people without high cholesterol
 jau main protein kii tulana main doguna fibre hota he, jo vajan niyantran yaa aahaar chintaaon kaa saamana kar rahe logon ke liye ek mahatvapurn he
 For this research, 14 studies were conducted on clinical trials in seven countries, including Canada
 tippaniyan This research has been published in the European Journal of Clinical Nutrition
 (is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he
 This is published directly from the Syndicate feed)
 shodh ke nateezon ke mutabik, sharir main kam-ghanatv vaale lypoprotein yani ldl or gaiyr-ucch ghanatv vaale lypoprotein yani non echdiel ko saat fisadi kam kar saktaa he
